# <a name="microsoft-365-encryption-chains"></a><span data-ttu-id="33d19-103">Catene di crittografia di Microsoft 365</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="33d19-103">Microsoft 365 encryption chains</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="33d19-104">Microsoft 365 sfrutta diversi provider di certificati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="33d19-104">Microsoft 365 leverages a number of different certificate providers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="33d19-105">Di seguito viene descritto l'elenco completo dei certificati radice di Microsoft 365 noti che i clienti possono riscontrare quando accedono a Microsoft 365.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="33d19-105">The following describes the complete list of known Microsoft 365 root certificates that customers may encounter when accessing Microsoft 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="33d19-106">Per informazioni sui certificati che potrebbe essere necessario installare nella propria infrastruttura, vedere Pianificare certificati SSL di terze parti [per Microsoft 365.](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/enterprise/plan-for-third-party-ssl-certificates)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="33d19-106">For information on the certificates you may need to install in your own infrastructure, see [Plan for third-party SSL certificates for Microsoft 365](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/enterprise/plan-for-third-party-ssl-certificates).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="33d19-107">Le seguenti informazioni sui certificati si applicano a tutte le istanze cloud nazionali e internazionali di Microsoft 365.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="33d19-107">The following certificate information applies to all worldwide and national cloud instances of Microsoft 365.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="33d19-108">Last updated: **16/10/2020**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="33d19-108">Last updated: **10/16/2020**</span></span>
